Emerging growth company </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="c-1" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox" id="f-22">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act.&#160;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#168;</span></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="height:42.75pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><span><br/></span></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:42.75pt;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div><div><span style="color:#5f0095;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:22pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item&#160;2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On September&#160;28, 2023, Accenture plc (&#8220;Accenture&#8221;) issued a news release announcing financial results for its fourth quarter and full fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2023.</span></div><div style="margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A copy of the news release is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;99. All information in the news release is furnished but not filed.</span></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Non-GAAP Financial Information</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the attached news release Accenture discloses the following non-GAAP financial measures:</span></div><div style="text-indent:24.75pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Free cash flow (defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions). Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this information provides meaningful additional information regarding the company&#8217;s liquidity. </span></div><div style="padding-left:72pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Percentage changes in revenues and bookings on a local currency basis. Financial results in local currency are calculated by restating current period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior year period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates. This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues. </span></div><div style="padding-left:72pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Adjusted financial measures excluding the impact of business optimization costs and gain on an investment. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding the effect of the business optimization costs and the investment gain facilitates an understanding as to the impact of these items and the company&#8217;s performance in comparison to the prior period.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this non-GAAP financial information is useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP.</span></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><span style="color:#5f0095;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:22pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item&#160;9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><span Board of Directors approves $4.0&#160;billion of additional share repurchase authority --</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- For fiscal year 2024, Accenture expects revenue growth of 2% to 5% in local currency&#59; GAAP diluted EPS of $11.41 to $11.76, a 6% to 9% increase&#59; and adjusted EPS of $11.97 to $12.32, a 3% to 6% increase --</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">NEW YORK&#59; September&#160;28, 2023 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE&#58; ACN) reported financial results for the fourth quarter and full fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2023. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">For the fourth quarter</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">, revenues were $16.0&#160;billion, an increase of 4% in both U.S. dollars and local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. GAAP operating income was $1.91&#160;billion, compared to $2.27 billion for the fourth quarter last year, and operating margin was 12.0% compared to 14.7% for the fourth quarter last year. Adjusted operating income was $2.38&#160;billion and adjusted operating margin was 14.9%, an expansion of 20 basis points from the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. GAAP diluted earnings per share were $2.15, compared to $2.60 for the fourth quarter last year. Adjusted EPS were $2.71, an increase of 4% from the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. Operating cash flow was $3.41&#160;billion and free cash flow was $3.23&#160;billion. New bookings were $16.6 billion. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">For the full fiscal year</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">, revenues were $64.1&#160;billion, an increase of 4% in U.S. dollars and 8% in local currency compared with fiscal 2022. GAAP operating income was $8.81&#160;billion, compared to $9.37 billion in fiscal 2022, and operating margin was 13.7% compared to 15.2% in fiscal 2022. Adjusted operating income was $9.87&#160;billion and adjusted operating margin was 15.4%, an expansion of 20 basis points from fiscal 2022. GAAP diluted earnings per share were $10.77, compared to $10.71 in fiscal 2022. Adjusted EPS were $11.67, an increase of 9% from fiscal 2022.  Operating cash flow was $9.52&#160;billion and free cash flow was $9.00&#160;billion. New bookings were $72.2&#160;billion.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.15pt;vertical-align:baseline">1</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted financial measures presented in this release are non-GAAP financial measures that exclude business optimization costs and a gain related to our investment in Duck Creek Technologies, as further described in this release.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:58.5pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Julie Sweet, chair and CEO, Accenture, said, &#8220;I am extremely proud that we have achieved another strong year of financial performance in fiscal year 2023. Our ability to remain laser-focused on meeting the needs of our clients is reflected in new bookings of $72&#160;billion in fiscal 2023&#59; 106 clients with quarterly bookings of more than $100 million&#59; and reaching a record 300 Diamond clients, our largest relationships. Our clients&#8217; generative AI bookings of $300 million in the last six months position us at the heart of the beginning of AI-fueled reinvention. I would like to thank our extraordinary </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">733,000</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> people who made these results possible and focus every day on creating 360&#176; value for all of our stakeholders.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Financial Review</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Fourth Quarter Fiscal 2023</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2023 were $15.99&#160;billion, compared with $15.42&#160;billion for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022, an increase of 4% in both U.S. dollars and local currency, and were within the company&#8217;s guided range of $15.75 billion to $16.35 billion. There was no foreign-exchange impact for the quarter, which was consistent with the assumption provided in the company&#8217;s third-quarter earnings release.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">Consulting revenues were $8.20 billion, a decrease of 2% in both U.S. dollars and local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">Managed Services revenues were $7.79&#160;billion, an increase of 10% in both U.S. dollars and local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted EPS for the quarter were $2.15 compared with $2.60 for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. Excluding a $0.56 decrease for business optimization costs, adjusted EPS were $2.71, an increase of 4% from the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. The $0.11 increase in EPS on an adjusted basis reflects&#58;</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">a $0.14 increase from higher revenue and operating results&#59; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">a $0.08 increase from higher non-operating income&#59; and</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">a $0.01 increase from lower share count&#59;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">partially offset by</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">a $0.11 decrease from a higher effective tax rate&#59; and</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">   </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">a $0.01 decrease from higher noncontrolling interests.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the fourth quarter was 32.4%,</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">compared with 32.1% for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. Selling, general and administrative (SG&#38;A) expenses for the fourth quarter were $2.80&#160;billion, or 17.5% of revenues, compared with $2.68&#160;billion, or 17.4% of revenues, for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP operating income for the quarter decreased 16%, to $1.91&#160;billion, or 12.0% of revenues, compared with $2.27&#160;billion, or 14.7% of revenues, for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. Adjusted </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:58.5pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">operating income for the quarter was $2.38&#160;billion, or 14.9% of revenues, an expansion of 20 basis points from the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company's GAAP effective tax rate for the quarter was 28.1%, compared with 24.6% for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. On an adjusted basis, the effective tax rate for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2023 was 27.4%. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP net income for the quarter was $1.41 billion, compared with $1.69 billion for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. $8.86&#160;billion, an increase of 10% in U.S. dollars and 15% in local currency compared with fiscal 2022.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Returning Cash to Shareholders</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture continues to return cash to shareholders through cash dividends and share repurchases. These cash dividend payments totaled </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">$706 million, bringing dividend payments for the full year to $2.83 billion, compared with $2.46&#160;billion in fiscal 2022. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture plc has declared a quarterly cash dividend of $1.29 per share, for shareholders of record at the close of business on October&#160;12, 2023. This dividend, which is payable on November&#160;15, 2023, represents a 15% increase over the company&#8217;s previous quarterly dividend.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Share Repurchase Activity</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">During the fourth quarter of fiscal 2023, Accenture repurchased or redeemed 3.2 million shares, including 3.1 million shares repurchased in the open market, for a total of $1.0&#160;billion. This brought total share repurchases and redemptions for the full fiscal year to 15.3 million shares, including 12.8 million shares repurchased in the open market, for a total of $4.3 billion. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">T</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">he company&#8217;s Board of Directors has approved $4.0&#160;billion in additional share repurchase authority, bringing Accenture&#8217;s total outstanding authority to approximately $6.5&#160;billion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">At August&#160;31, 2023, Accenture had approximately 629</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">million total shares outstanding.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Business Outlook</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">First Quarter Fiscal 2024</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Accenture expects revenues for the first quarter of fiscal 2024 to be in the range of $15.85&#160;billion to $16.45&#160;billion, or -2% to 2% in local currency, reflecting the company&#8217;s assumption of a positive 2.5% foreign-exchange impact compared with the first quarter of fiscal 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Fiscal Year 2024</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">&#160;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture&#8217;s business outlook for the full 2024 fiscal year assumes that the foreign-exchange impact on its results in U.S. dollars will be flat compared with fiscal 2023. For fiscal 2024, the company expects revenue growth to be in the range of 2% to 5% in local currency. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:58.5pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture expects GAAP operating margin for fiscal 2024 to be in the range of 14.8% to </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">15.0%, an expansion of 110 to 130 basis points from fiscal 2023, and adjusted operating margin, which excludes an estimated $450 million for business optimization costs, to be in the range of 15.5% to 15.7%, an expansion of 10 to 30 basis points from fiscal 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company expects both its GAAP and adjusted annual effective tax rate, which excludes the tax impacts of business optimization costs, to be in the range of 23.5% to 25.5%.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company expects GAAP diluted EPS to be in the range of $11.41 to $11.76, an increase of 6% to 9% over fiscal 2023 and adjusted EPS to be in the range of $11.97 to $12.32, an increase of 3% to 6% over fiscal 2023. This excludes $0.56 for business optimization costs in fiscal 2024.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For fiscal 2024, the company expects operating cash flow to be in the range of $9.3&#160;billion to $9.9&#160;billion&#59; property and equipment additions to be $600&#160;million&#59; and free cash flow to be in the range of $8.7&#160;billion to $9.3&#160;billion.&#160; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company expects to return at least $7.7 billion in cash to shareholders through dividends and share repurchases.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">360&#176; Value Reporting</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture&#8217;s goal is to create 360&#176; value for our clients, people, shareholders, partners, and communities.
